function kill_vanya ()
local npc = level_object_by_sid (043)
if npc == nil then
return
end
local h = hit()
h.power = 100
h.direction = npc:direction()
h.draftsman = npc
h.impulse = 1
h.type = hit.wound
npc:hit(h)
end
